This is a nice paved, 2 lane bike/run/walk trail with a few side trails that lead to small parks with drinking fountains. While the parks are not initialy visible from the main bike trail, they are nice when you need a water stop on longer runs to refill your bottles. I can easily turn an out and back into a 13.1 mile training run.< /Review>

<Rate>5</Rate>< text>
Wow! If you haven't been out to the Miner's Ravine Trail in a while (or ever) then I HIGHLY SUGGEST getting over to Roseville to  check it out!!!
Roseville has gone above and beyond and spared no expense on this trail. This trail is beautiful!
I only stumbled upon it when I lost my kitty and various leads to her whereabouts sent me towards the Miner's Ravine Trail.
So, next time you have out-of-town guests, or feel like just getting out for some fresh air, look no further than your own backyard. Great Trail for all ages, hiking or biking.
Please don't litter and keep an eye out for my furbaby, Sisssta! Not going to stop looking until I find her. Thank you...‚ù£< /text>

< text>
Cave Campground ($16 per night) is a very nice campground during off-peak days, but its biggest drawback is the traffic noise. You will hear very loud road noise all night long. In addition, there aren't sinks and there didn't seem to be convenient water. In October it gets very cold at night. On the plus side, the campground has very spacious campsites, and you don't really have to see or hear other people very much at all.</text>

Cindy Vogel<//user_name>
< text>
Really like this campground. They allow tents. It's pretty. They have bathrooms and they are cleanish.  The road is noisy but not entirely awful. Good fishing and the sound of Hat Creek. Lovely. 3 stars because our campsite had all sorts of dog poop and litter. The barbecue was dirty and the women's bathroom had no lights the first 3 nights of our stay. The camp authority was quick to tell us we couldn't use the electricity in our campsite because it belonged to the camp host. Why the camp host was not camped here is beyond me. Those iPhones really can put a drain on that government bill. They were, however, not so quick enforcing leash rules or the 9:00 PM quiet rule. We were verbally threated by drunk adults and their awful  children. The camp host did nothing.  They need to identify campsite spots, post rules and take advantage of signage. And put the camp host in his spot. Unless of course, he was in his spot, as the signage implied. I think they were just throwing their "all important " selves around.</text>

Good  perfec< /Text>
<Pics>None</Pics><response>None<//response><GmapID>0x80c2cd203c47f555:0x7eec3ed5cf91cfec<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>
< user_id>
103548908178775208739< /user_id>
< Name>
Roberto Terriquez<//Name>
< Time>
1478038035648</Time>
<Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
I grew up in this town. I left this place in the late 80s so I didn't  know where to find good places to eat around here anymore. My family referred me to this place so I checked it out. I went on a Sunday and they had a live Sinaloense band playing. It was like walking into banda club. The music was a bit loud. Everyone looked at me like I was out of place. I guess everyone knows the regulars here. No one tried to intimidate me or stare me down though. The waitresses were really nice. They had an assorted menu to choose from. I had their shrimp coctel and a couple of ceviche tostadas and a michelada. Their coctel was great. Their ceviche tostadas were also great. They serve their micheladas in a large caguama (family size if you are not familiar with the term) size Styrofoam cup with ice in it. I have never been served a michelada like this before. At first I thought, this michelada is going to suck. Beer is nasty with ice in it. Man was I in for a surprise. The michelada was the best michelada I had in my life! I am not exaggerating. I have had plenty of micheladas and this one was the best tasting one hands down. After having two of the micheladas the music wasn't so loud anymore. In fact, the music was not as loud as I would have liked it to be. I was having a blast with my family. I had dancing feet listening to the new school sinaloense banda music. I grew up listening to the old school Jalisco bandas like Banda Machos, Banda Cuisillos, Banda Pelillos and others. Good music is good music. These guys were killing it with the music.

In the end, I enjoyed the visit here. The tab for four people's meals and beers and a bucket of beer I treated a nearby table to was less than one hundred bucks. You can't beat that. I will definitely visit this place again when I am in town. I highly recommend giving this place a try.< /Review>
